CREATE TABLE courses (
  id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
  course_code VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  course_num VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  course_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  days VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  start_time TIME NOT NULL,
  end_time TIME NOT NULL,
  professor VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  professor_rate DECIMAL(3,1) NOT NULL,
  professor_lev_diff DECIMAL(3,1) NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE schedule_courses (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INT NOT NULL,
    course_code VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    course_num VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    course_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    days VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    start_time TIME NOT NULL,
    end_time TIME NOT NULL,
    professor VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    professor_rate DECIMAL(3,2) NOT NULL,
    professor_lev_diff DECIMAL(3,2) NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    UNIQUE (course_code, course_num, course_name)
);
